<script type="text/javascript">
	function loadJSAsync( ) {
		for ( var i = 0; i < arguments.length; i++ ) {
			var url = arguments[i];
			(function() {
				var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
				s.async = true;
				s.src = url;
				el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
			})();
		}
	}
</script>

<div id="u_nav">
    <script>

function regExpEscape(s) {
    return String(s).replace(/([-()\[\]{}+?*.$\^|,:#<!\\])/g, '\\$1').
            replace(/\x08/g, '\\x08');
}


function appendParamsOnce(url, params) {
    var useParams = params.replace(/^(\?|\&)/, '');
    if (url.match(new RegExp('[\\?|\\&]' + regExpEscape(useParams))) == null) {
        return url += (url.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?' ) + useParams;
    }
    return url;
}

</script>

<b class="jobtitle"><font size="+1">Automation Engineer</font></b>

<br>
<span class="company">Lenze Americas</span>
    <a data-tn-element="reviewStars" data-tn-variant="vjreviews" class="turnstileLink slNoUnderline " href="/cmp/Lenze-Americas/reviews"  class="ratingsLabel" onmousedown="this.href = appendParamsOnce(this.href, '?campaignid=vjreviews&from=viewjob&jt=Automation+Engineer&fromjk=3ef9910afb3c013a');" target="_blank"

    <table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 border=0><tr><td class="snip">
<span id="job_summary" class="summary"><p><b>Lenze</b> is a global manufacturer of electrical and mechanical drives, motion control and automation technology offering products, drive solutions, complete automation systems, and engineering services and tools from one single source. We are able to support the customer throughout the entire machine development process from the control system to the drive shaft, from the initial idea to after-sales.</p><p>Our products can be found in many industries, including automotive, packaging, material handling and logistics, robotics, and commercial equipment (pumps/fans). A global network of distributors and representatives makes Lenze Americas perfectly positioned to meet the motion control needs of customers worldwide. Lenze Americas, the American subsidiary of Lenze SE of Germany, is headquartered in Uxbridge, Massachusetts; corporate global headquarters are in Hamelin, Germany.</p><p>The <b>Automation Engineer</b> will support our Solution and System Sales force in the Pre-Sales phase to win new Lenze Automation Solutions and Systems. Project Implementation. Help to achieve our Lenze Americas Solution and System revenue target.</p><p><b>Key Responsibilities Include</b></p><p>The <b>Automation Engineer</b> will be assigned to the Solution and System Application Team. Support our Solution and System Sales force in the Pre-Sales phase to win new Lenze Automation Solutions and Systems. Project Implementation. Help to achieve our Lenze Americas Solution and System revenue target.</p><ul><li>Machine Assessment</li><li>Create Machine Specification</li><li>Sizing / Selecting</li><li>Develop Value Proposal</li><li>Present our Automation Solution and System</li><li>Provide Support to Sales in Solution quote creation</li><li>Provide technical advice to our Customers and Sales</li><li>Develop customer PLC and HMI software</li><li>Commissioning of Lenze Solutions and Systems</li><li>Automation project support via phone, remote desktop and onsite.</li><li>Internal and external Automation, Solution and System training.</li><li>Provide sales support to field sales, this includes regional training as well as sales support calls</li><li>Project management</li><li>Help to grow our Automation solution revenue</li></ul><p><b>Requirements</b></p><ul><li>Bachelor degree required in Electrical, Mechatronics or Robotics</li><li>8+ Years in the area mentioned above</li><li>IEC 61131-3 (Ladder, Structure text, Function block diagram)</li><li>HMI programming</li><li>Fieldbus (Ethercat, CAN, Ethernet-IP, RS232/485)</li><li>Mechatronic (Mechanic/Electric/Software)</li><li>Machine commissioning</li><li>Machine assessment</li><li>Creating Application / Machine specification</li><li>Familiar with wiring diagrams and troubleshooting customer wiring</li><li>Project management</li><li>Software, installation and setup support on windows systems(would be helpful)</li></ul><p><b>Benefits</b></p><p>Lenze values supporting our employees and our communities. We offer a comprehensive benefits program and a work environment designed to support you and your family. Here is an overview of the benefits you can look forward to receiving while working at Lenze:</p><ul><li>Health & Wellness: Medical, Dental, Vision, Prescription Drug, FSA</li><li>Financial: 401(k), Tuition Assistance</li><li>Supplemental: Life and AD&D, Voluntary Life and AD&D, Disability, Accident, Critical Illness</li><li>Lifestyle: Paid Time Off, Annual Employee Appreciation Event and many other Employee Events!</li></ul><p>Supporting our communities, both locally and globally, is core to Lenze. This includes activities with food pantries, Toys for Tots, Salvation Army, Read Across America, American Red Cross, and much more!</p><p>Job Type: Full-time</p></span><br><div id="p_3ef9910afb3c013a">

	function loadJSAsync( ) {
		for ( var i = 0; i < arguments.length; i++ ) {
			var url = arguments[i];
			(function() {
				var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
				s.async = true;
				s.src = url;
				el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
			})();
		}
	}
</script>

<div id="u_nav">
    <script>

function regExpEscape(s) {
    return String(s).replace(/([-()\[\]{}+?*.$\^|,:#<!\\])/g, '\\$1').
            replace(/\x08/g, '\\x08');
}


function appendParamsOnce(url, params) {
    var useParams = params.replace(/^(\?|\&)/, '');
    if (url.match(new RegExp('[\\?|\\&]' + regExpEscape(useParams))) == null) {
        return url += (url.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?' ) + useParams;
    }
    return url;
}

</script>

	function loadJSAsync( ) {
		for ( var i = 0; i < arguments.length; i++ ) {
			var url = arguments[i];
			(function() {
				var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
				s.async = true;
				s.src = url;
				el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
			})();
		}
	}
</script>

<div id="u_nav">
    <script>

function regExpEscape(s) {
    return String(s).replace(/([-()\[\]{}+?*.$\^|,:#<!\\])/g, '\\$1').
            replace(/\x08/g, '\\x08');
}


function appendParamsOnce(url, params) {
    var useParams = params.replace(/^(\?|\&)/, '');
    if (url.match(new RegExp('[\\?|\\&]' + regExpEscape(useParams))) == null) {
        return url += (url.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?' ) + useParams;
    }
    return url;
}

</script>

<div data-tn-component="jobHeader">
<b class="jobtitle"><font size="+1">Mechanical Systems Design (multiple openings)</font></b>

<br>
<span class="company">The Structures Company, LLC</span>
     -
<span class="location">United States</span>
    <div>
        <span class="no-wrap">Contract</span>
        </div>

    <table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 border=0><tr><td class="snip">
<span id="job_summary" class="summary"><p><b>Mechanical Systems Design (multiple openings)</b></p><p>Location: North Carolina</p><p>Duration: long term contract, 12+ months</p><p>Rate: Open, DOE</p><p>Overtime</p><p><b>Mechanical Systems Design Engineer Summary</b></p><ul><li>Perform preliminary and detail design of aircraft mechanical systems, including flight controls, hydraulic systems and ECS systems.</li><li>Create 3D/2D definition.</li><li>CATIA V5 is a plus.</li><li>Participate in the Engineering definition review, approval and release process</li><li>Support the review of manufacturing plans and procedures to ensure compliance with design requirements</li><li>Can possess background in aircraft structural design as well.</li></ul><p><b>Mechanical Systems Education, Work Experience, Certification and/or Licensure</b> :</p><p>1. Bachelor’s degree in engineering or equivalent years of work experience in lieu of formal education.</p><p>2. Structural analysis certification to Part 23 or 25 standards.</p><p><b>Mechanical Systems Design Knowledge, Skills and Abilities: </b></p><p>1. Strong oral an written communication skills.</p><p>2. Ability to multitask.</p><p>3. Ability work independently as well as in a mutli-functional team environment.</p><p>4. Working knowledge of Microsoft Office (Word, Excel, and PowerPoint).5. Extensive working knowledge and experience with CATIA v.5.</p><p>6. Visual Basic, Matlab, Simulink, FiberSim, Determinent Assembly techniques, composite curing, and Geometric Dimensioning and Tolerance experience preferred.</p><p>7. Knowledge of principles of structural design mechanics including predicting strength and other possible structural instabilities.</p><p>8. Prior experience in FEM analysis preferred.</p><p>9. Strong mechanical design skills for all structural components of aircraft.</p><p><b>Mechanical Systems Design Physical Requirements</b> :</p><p>1. Incumbents may be routinely exposed to equipment operational noise heat-cold-dust, and/or aircraft equipment, parts, or fuel odors.</p><p>2. Incumbents may be required to stand, sit, squat, walk, bend, climb ladders, move, reach, or stretch for prolonged time periods with no restrictions, as required by job duties.</p><p>3. Work in a safe and professional manner while adhering to all regulatory requirements (FAA, OSHA, DOT, EPA, State, and Federal regulations, etc.).</p><p>4. Read, hear, speak, and see with no restrictions, as required by job duties.</p><p>5. Comprehend and adhere to management directions and/or safety instructions with no restrictions.</p><p>6. Effectively communicate in Business English language.</p><p>7. Pull, push, carry, lift, or move items up to 10 lbs. throughout the work shift without assistance, as required by job duties.</p><p>8. Pull, push, carry, lift or move materials/people/items/equipment weighing up to 50lbs or more during the work shift, with the use of Company provided “reach assistance technology” or “movement assist technology” (fork-lifts, pallet jacks, pulleys, dolly’s, robotics reach equipment, people movers etc.), as required by job duties.</p><p>Job Type: Contract</p></span><br><div id="p_9c465f9232dc05ec">

	function loadJSAsync( ) {
		for ( var i = 0; i < arguments.length; i++ ) {
			var url = arguments[i];
			(function() {
				var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
				s.async = true;
				s.src = url;
				el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
			})();
		}
	}
</script>

<div id="u_nav">
    <script>

function regExpEscape(s) {
    return String(s).replace(/([-()\[\]{}+?*.$\^|,:#<!\\])/g, '\\$1').
            replace(/\x08/g, '\\x08');
}


function appendParamsOnce(url, params) {
    var useParams = params.replace(/^(\?|\&)/, '');
    if (url.match(new RegExp('[\\?|\\&]' + regExpEscape(useParams))) == null) {
        return url += (url.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?' ) + useParams;
    }
    return url;
}

</script>

<span id="job_summary" class="summary"><p><b>********** Requires APPLIED MATERIALS Experience *********</b></p><p><b>Amat Equipment Service / Field Service Engineer / Tool Owner</b></p><p><b>Job Summary: </b></p><p>He will be responsible for maintenance, repair, refurbishment, installation, and filed service of semiconductor manufacturing equipment.</p><p><b>Responsibilities: </b></p><ul><li>Provide technical and hands-on service of Applied Materials "Amat" Centura and P5000 systems</li><li>Work independently, performs complex duties in the refurbishment, repair, trouble-shoot, and installation of semiconductor manufacturing equipment.</li><li>Dismantle, adjust, and repair equipment according to maintenance specifications and repair manuals.</li><li>Use schematics, hand tools, electrical gauges and common test equipment for calibration, diagnosis and repair of equipment.</li><li>Perform electrical, mechanical or software troubleshooting to determine problems in non-functioning equipment.</li><li>Installation of semiconductor equipment in customer facilities world-wide.</li><li>Provide detailed pass-downs regarding daily issues and activities.</li><li>Identify opportunities to improve manufacturing workflow.</li><li>Commit to creating and maintaining a safe work environment.</li><li>Knowledge of electronics, mechanics, robotics, hydraulics, test equipment, pneumatics and vacuum system.</li><li>Must be able to follow complex technical written and verbal instructions. Requires strong interpersonal skills.</li><li>Must be able to lift up to 50 lbs and have a valid US driver’s license.</li><li>Provide leadership to other technicians by providing training and mentoring.</li><li>Hands-on and creative individual with willingness to work independently in a cleanroom environment.</li><li>High level of attention to detail.</li><li>‪Methodical approach to troubleshooting and project management.</li><li>‪Good written and verbal communication skills.</li><li>‪Self-motivated; ability to work independently under general guidance and direction.</li><li>‪Ability to independently learn systems and processes associated with the position.</li></ul><p><b>Education & Experience: </b></p><p>Minimum 3-5 years of Semiconductor Maintenance experience.</p><p>Experience with at least one of the following tool sets are</p><p><b>Required: </b> Amat Centura, Amat P5000</p><p><b>Plus: </b> Amat Endura, Amat Producer.</p><p>‪Practical knowledge of Electro-Mechanical manufacturing processes (machining, welding, soldering) is a plus.</p><p>Relocation assistance available.</p><p>Travel is required.</p><p>Basic wage + Quarterly bonus</p><p>Job Type: Full-time</p><p>Salary: $30.00 to $40.00 /hour</p><p>Required education:</p><ul><li>High school or equivalent</li></ul><p>Required experience:</p><ul><li>Amat Centura or P5000: 2 years</li></ul><p>Required license or certification:</p><ul><li>Driver's License</li></ul><p>Required travel:</p><ul><li>25%</li></ul></span><br><div id="p_d280cde49f1916a2">

if (window.addEventListener) {

} else if (window.attachEvent) {
window.attachEvent('onmessage', icims_handlePostMessage);
}
function icims_handlePostMessage(event) {
// If this is not a message from an icims domain, ignore it.
if (event.origin.indexOf('icims.com', event.origin.length - 9) == -1) return;
var data = null;
try {
data = ICIMS.jsonDecode(event.data);
} catch(e) {}
if (data == null && event.data != null) data = event.data;
try {
if ('height' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['height'])) {
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').height = parseInt(data['height']) + 60;
}
} else if ('x' in data && 'y' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['x']) && !isNaN(data['y'])) {
top.scrollTo(parseInt(data['x']), parseInt(data['y']));
}
}
} catch (e) {}
}
function getCookie(name) {
var match = document.cookie.match(name + '=(.*?)(;|$)');
if (match) return unescape(match[1]);
else return "";
}
function updateUrl(url) {
try {
history.replaceState({}, '', url);
} catch (e) {}
}

<script type="text/javascript" src="https://cdn07.icims.com/a/images.icims.com/content/platform_104.1.171030.1509383491/script/lib/domreplacement/domReplacement.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://cdn07.icims.com/a/images.icims.com/content/platform_104.1.171030.1509383491/script/common/icims.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://cdn07.icims.com/a/images.icims.com/content/platform_104.1.171030.1509383491/script/portal/utils.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">var useAutoScrolling = false;</script>
<!--[if lte IE 8]>
<script type="text/javascript">useAutoScrolling = true;</script>
<![endif]-->
<script type="text/javascript">

if (window.addEventListener) {
window.addEventListener('message', icims_handlePostMessage, false);
} else if (window.attachEvent) {
window.attachEvent('onmessage', icims_handlePostMessage);
}
function icims_handlePostMessage(event) {
// If this is not a message from an icims domain, ignore it.
if (event.origin.indexOf('icims.com', event.origin.length - 9) == -1) return;
var data = null;
try {
data = ICIMS.jsonDecode(event.data);
} catch(e) {}
if (data == null && event.data != null) data = event.data;
try {
if ('height' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['height'])) {
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').height = parseInt(data['height']) + 60;
}
} else if ('x' in data && 'y' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['x']) && !isNaN(data['y'])) {
top.scrollTo(parseInt(data['x']), parseInt(data['y']));
}
}
} catch (e) {}
}
function getCookie(name) {
var match = document.cookie.match(name + '=(.*?)(;|$)');
if (match) return unescape(match[1]);
else return "";
}
function updateUrl(url) {
try {
history.replaceState({}, '', url);
} catch (e) {}
}
icimsAddOnload(function() {
var icimsFrame = document.createElement('iframe');
var iFrameHeight = 500;
icimsFrame.id = 'icims_content_iframe';
icimsFrame.name = 'icims_content_iframe';
icimsFrame.src = 'https:\/\/us-amazon.icims.com\/jobs\/564422\/hardware-support-engineer\/job?iis=Job+Posting&iisn=Indeed+%28Paid+Sponsored+Posting%29&in_iframe=1';
icimsFrame.setAttribute('width', '100%');


iFrameHeight = 1200;

icimsFrame.setAttribute('height', iFrameHeight);

if (!useAutoScrolling && window.postMessage) {
icimsFrame.setAttribute('scrolling', 'no');
} else {
icimsFrame.setAttribute('scrolling', 'auto');
}
icimsFrame.setAttribute('title', 'iCIMS Content iFrame');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('marginwidth', '0');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('marginheight', '0');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('frameborder', '0');
icimsFrame.onload=function() {
try {
window.parent.parent.scrollTo(0,0);
} catch (e) {}
};
document.getElementById('icims_iframe_span').appendChild(icimsFrame);
try {
var height = getCookie('cookie_icims_iframe_content_height');
if (height > 0) style.height = height + 'px';
} catch(e) {}
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').onreadystatechange = function() {
try{
if ('interactive' == this.readyState) {
window.scroll(1,1);
}
} catch(e) {}
};
try {
var height = 0;
if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Firefox")!=-1) height = document.body.offsetHeight + 16;
else height = document.body.scrollHeight;
document.cookie="cookie_icims_iframe_content_height="+height+"; path=/;";
} catch(e) {}
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

if (window.addEventListener) {
window.addEventListener('message', icims_handlePostMessage, false);
} else if (window.attachEvent) {
window.attachEvent('onmessage', icims_handlePostMessage);
}
function icims_handlePostMessage(event) {
// If this is not a message from an icims domain, ignore it.
if (event.origin.indexOf('icims.com', event.origin.length - 9) == -1) return;
var data = null;
try {
data = ICIMS.jsonDecode(event.data);
} catch(e) {}
if (data == null && event.data != null) data = event.data;
try {
if ('height' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['height'])) {
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').height = parseInt(data['height']) + 60;
}
} else if ('x' in data && 'y' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['x']) && !isNaN(data['y'])) {
top.scrollTo(parseInt(data['x']), parseInt(data['y']));
}
}
} catch (e) {}
}
function getCookie(name) {
var match = document.cookie.match(name + '=(.*?)(;|$)');
if (match) return unescape(match[1]);
else return "";
}
function updateUrl(url) {
try {
history.replaceState({}, '', url);
} catch (e) {}
}
icimsAddOnload(function() {
var icimsFrame = document.createElement('iframe');
var iFrameHeight = 500;
icimsFrame.id = 'icims_content_iframe';
icimsFrame.name = 'icims_content_iframe';
icimsFrame.src = 'https:\/\/us-amazon.icims.com\/jobs\/594959\/principal-technical-program-manager%2c-robotics\/job?iis=Job+Posting&iisn=Indeed+%28Paid+Sponsored+Posting%29&in_iframe=1';
icimsFrame.setAttribute('width', '100%');


iFrameHeight = 1200;

icimsFrame.setAttribute('height', iFrameHeight);

if (!useAutoScrolling && window.postMessage) {
icimsFrame.setAttribute('scrolling', 'no');
} else {
icimsFrame.setAttribute('scrolling', 'auto');
}
icimsFrame.setAttribute('title', 'iCIMS Content iFrame');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('marginwidth', '0');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('marginheight', '0');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('frameborder', '0');
icimsFrame.onload=function() {
try {
window.parent.parent.scrollTo(0,0);
} catch (e) {}
};
document.getElementById('icims_iframe_span').appendChild(icimsFrame);
try {
var height = getCookie('cookie_icims_iframe_content_height');
if (height > 0) style.height = height + 'px';
} catch(e) {}
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').onreadystatechange = function() {
try{
if ('interactive' == this.readyState) {
window.scroll(1,1);
}
} catch(e) {}
};
try {
var height = 0;
if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Firefox")!=-1) height = document.body.offsetHeight + 16;
else height = document.body.scrollHeight;
document.cookie="cookie_icims_iframe_content_height="+height+"; path=/;";
} catch(e) {}
});

function icims_handlePostMessage(event) {
// If this is not a message from an icims domain, ignore it.
if (event.origin.indexOf('icims.com', event.origin.length - 9) == -1) return;
var data = null;
try {
data = ICIMS.jsonDecode(event.data);
} catch(e) {}
if (data == null && event.data != null) data = event.data;
try {
if ('height' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['height'])) {
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').height = parseInt(data['height']) + 60;
}
} else if ('x' in data && 'y' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['x']) && !isNaN(data['y'])) {
top.scrollTo(parseInt(data['x']), parseInt(data['y']));
}
}
} catch (e) {}
}
function getCookie(name) {
var match = document.cookie.match(name + '=(.*?)(;|$)');
if (match) return unescape(match[1]);
else return "";
}
function updateUrl(url) {
try {
history.replaceState({}, '', url);
} catch (e) {}
}
icimsAddOnload(function() {
var icimsFrame = document.createElement('iframe');
var iFrameHeight = 500;
icimsFrame.id = 'icims_content_iframe';
icimsFrame.name = 'icims_content_iframe';
icimsFrame.src = 'https:\/\/us-amazon.icims.com\/jobs\/594407\/senior-software-development-engineer\/job?iis=Job+Posting&iisn=Indeed+%28Paid+Sponsored+Posting%29&in_iframe=1';
icimsFrame.setAttribute('width', '100%');


iFrameHeight = 1200;

icimsFrame.setAttribute('height', iFrameHeight);

if (!useAutoScrolling && window.postMessage) {
icimsFrame.setAttribute('scrolling', 'no');
} else {
icimsFrame.setAttribute('scrolling', 'auto');
}
icimsFrame.setAttribute('title', 'iCIMS Content iFrame');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('marginwidth', '0');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('marginheight', '0');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('frameborder', '0');
icimsFrame.onload=function() {
try {
window.parent.parent.scrollTo(0,0);
} catch (e) {}
};
document.getElementById('icims_iframe_span').appendChild(icimsFrame);
try {
var height = getCookie('cookie_icims_iframe_content_height');
if (height > 0) style.height = height + 'px';
} catch(e) {}
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').onreadystatechange = function() {
try{
if ('interactive' == this.readyState) {
window.scroll(1,1);
}
} catch(e) {}
};
try {
var height = 0;
if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Firefox")!=-1) height = document.body.offsetHeight + 16;
else height = document.body.scrollHeight;
document.cookie="cookie_icims_iframe_content_height="+height+"; path=/;";
} catch(e) {}
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" src="https://cdn07.icims.com/a/images.icims.com/content/platform_104.1.171030.1509383491/script/lib/domreplacement/domReplacement.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://cdn07.icims.com/a/images.icims.com/content/platform_104.1.171030.1509383491/script/common/icims.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://cdn07.icims.com/a/images.icims.com/content/platform_104.1.171030.1509383491/script/portal/utils.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">var useAutoScrolling = false;</script>
<!--[if lte IE 8]>
<script type="text/javascript">useAutoScrolling = true;</script>
<![endif]-->
<script type="text/javascript">

if (window.addEventListener) {
window.addEventListener('message', icims_handlePostMessage, false);
} else if (window.attachEvent) {
window.attachEvent('onmessage', icims_handlePostMessage);
}
function icims_handlePostMessage(event) {
// If this is not a message from an icims domain, ignore it.
if (event.origin.indexOf('icims.com', event.origin.length - 9) == -1) return;
var data = null;
try {
data = ICIMS.jsonDecode(event.data);
} catch(e) {}
if (data == null && event.data != null) data = event.data;
try {
if ('height' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['height'])) {
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').height = parseInt(data['height']) + 60;
}
} else if ('x' in data && 'y' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['x']) && !isNaN(data['y'])) {
top.scrollTo(parseInt(data['x']), parseInt(data['y']));
}
}
} catch (e) {}
}
function getCookie(name) {
var match = document.cookie.match(name + '=(.*?)(;|$)');
if (match) return unescape(match[1]);
else return "";
}
function updateUrl(url) {
try {
history.replaceState({}, '', url);
} catch (e) {}
}
icimsAddOnload(function() {
var icimsFrame = document.createElement('iframe');
var iFrameHeight = 500;
icimsFrame.id = 'icims_content_iframe';
icimsFrame.name = 'icims_content_iframe';
icimsFrame.src = 'https:\/\/us-amazon.icims.com\/jobs\/560197\/2018-boston-software-development-engineer-intern\/job?iis=Job+Posting&iisn=Indeed+%28Paid+Sponsored+Posting%29&in_iframe=1';
icimsFrame.setAttribute('width', '100%');


iFrameHeight = 1200;

icimsFrame.setAttribute('height', iFrameHeight);

if (!useAutoScrolling && window.postMessage) {
icimsFrame.setAttribute('scrolling', 'no');
} else {
icimsFrame.setAttribute('scrolling', 'auto');
}
icimsFrame.setAttribute('title', 'iCIMS Content iFrame');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('marginwidth', '0');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('marginheight', '0');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('frameborder', '0');
icimsFrame.onload=function() {
try {
window.parent.parent.scrollTo(0,0);
} catch (e) {}
};
document.getElementById('icims_iframe_span').appendChild(icimsFrame);
try {
var height = getCookie('cookie_icims_iframe_content_height');
if (height > 0) style.height = height + 'px';
} catch(e) {}
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').onreadystatechange = function() {
try{
if ('interactive' == this.readyState) {
window.scroll(1,1);
}
} catch(e) {}
};
try {
var height = 0;
if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Firefox")!=-1) height = document.body.offsetHeight + 16;
else height = document.body.scrollHeight;
document.cookie="cookie_icims_iframe_content_height="+height+"; path=/;";
} catch(e) {}
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

if (window.addEventListener) {
window.addEventListener('message', icims_handlePostMessage, false);
} else if (window.attachEvent) {
window.attachEvent('onmessage', icims_handlePostMessage);
}
function icims_handlePostMessage(event) {
// If this is not a message from an icims domain, ignore it.
if (event.origin.indexOf('icims.com', event.origin.length - 9) == -1) return;
var data = null;
try {
data = ICIMS.jsonDecode(event.data);
} catch(e) {}
if (data == null && event.data != null) data = event.data;
try {
if ('height' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['height'])) {
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').height = parseInt(data['height']) + 60;
}
} else if ('x' in data && 'y' in data) {
if (!isNaN(data['x']) && !isNaN(data['y'])) {
top.scrollTo(parseInt(data['x']), parseInt(data['y']));
}
}
} catch (e) {}
}
function getCookie(name) {
var match = document.cookie.match(name + '=(.*?)(;|$)');
if (match) return unescape(match[1]);
else return "";
}
function updateUrl(url) {
try {
history.replaceState({}, '', url);
} catch (e) {}
}
icimsAddOnload(function() {
var icimsFrame = document.createElement('iframe');
var iFrameHeight = 500;
icimsFrame.id = 'icims_content_iframe';
icimsFrame.name = 'icims_content_iframe';
icimsFrame.src = 'https:\/\/us-amazon.icims.com\/jobs\/557513\/software-development-engineer\/job?iis=Job+Posting&iisn=Indeed+%28Paid+Sponsored+Posting%29&in_iframe=1';
icimsFrame.setAttribute('width', '100%');


iFrameHeight = 1200;

icimsFrame.setAttribute('height', iFrameHeight);

if (!useAutoScrolling && window.postMessage) {
icimsFrame.setAttribute('scrolling', 'no');
} else {
icimsFrame.setAttribute('scrolling', 'auto');
}
icimsFrame.setAttribute('title', 'iCIMS Content iFrame');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('marginwidth', '0');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('marginheight', '0');
icimsFrame.setAttribute('frameborder', '0');
icimsFrame.onload=function() {
try {
window.parent.parent.scrollTo(0,0);
} catch (e) {}
};
document.getElementById('icims_iframe_span').appendChild(icimsFrame);
try {
var height = getCookie('cookie_icims_iframe_content_height');
if (height > 0) style.height = height + 'px';
} catch(e) {}
document.getElementById('icims_content_iframe').onreadystatechange = function() {
try{
if ('interactive' == this.readyState) {
window.scroll(1,1);
}
} catch(e) {}
};
try {
var height = 0;
if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Firefox")!=-1) height = document.body.offsetHeight + 16;
else height = document.body.scrollHeight;
document.cookie="cookie_icims_iframe_content_height="+height+"; path=/;";
} catch(e) {}
});
</script>
